Youth for Understanding has a young lady from India who had been placed for with a host family, and her host family needed to make a change. We are looking for a new host family (single, couple, family). Would you be willing to share her profile with friends who may be interested? Host families must speak English in the home, provide a bed in a bedroom, three meals per day and the love and support of a family. Lavanya comes with her own health insurance and spending money and YFU provides you a trained volunteer, orientations and 24-7 emergency support. Seventeen-year-old Lavanya comes from a village of 300 in India where her parents are agricultural laborers. She considers herself fortunate to have earned a position in an all girls school where she can receive an education. Lavanya dreams of college and a job in the Indian Administration Service, which would enable her to aid communities just like her own. \"There are green elds and water ow from small streams,\" she writes lovingly, adding that she wants to make a good name for her parents by helping the poor and increasing literacy. \"If every individual is happy,\" she believes, \"the world will be happy.\" Before school, Lavanya ambitiously wakes up at 5:00 am to exercise, run, bathe, and study before breakfast. After classes, she helps keep her school clean and neat. She and her friends spend free time discussing their futures, helping each other with academic problems, playing games, dancing, and singing. வருவதற்கான வாய்ப்புகள் உள்ளது கண்டறியப்பட்டது.குளத்தின் நீர்ப்பிடிப்பு பகுதியானது சுற்றுவட்டாரப் பகுதிகளில் உள்ள விவசாய நிலங்களே என்பதும் கண்டறியப்பட்டது.நீர்வரும் முக்கிய வாய்க்கால்கள் நன்றாக உள்ளது.அந்த முக்கிய வாய்க்காலுக்கு நீரைத்தரும் கிளை வாய்க்கால்கள் அதாவது விவசாய நிலங்கள், குடியிருப்பு பகுதிகள் மற்றும் சாலை ஓரங்களில் உள்ள வாய்க்கால்கள் ஆங்காங்கே தடுக்கப்பட்டுள்ளன.அவற்றை சரிசெய்தால் குளத்திற்கு நிச்சயமாக நீரை கொண்டு வந்து சேர்க்க முடியும்.\n\nஅந்த வழித்தடங்களை சீரமைக்க அரசு நிர்வாகங்களிடமிருந்து தேவையான அனுமதியைப் பெற்று, நிதி மற்றும் அதற்கான ஆதாரங்கள் குறித்து திட்டமிடப்பட்டு REGISTRATION BEFORE THE BEGINNING OF FALL SPORTS!*** FinalForms Athlete Online Registration All Hartford student-athletes are required to be registered in our online registration program. We are very excited to announce that the Hartford High School Athletic Department has partnered with FinalForms, an online forms and data management service. FinalForms allows you to complete and sign athletic participation forms for your students online. The most exciting news is that FinalForms saves data from season-to-season and year-to-year, meaning that you will never need to enter the same information twice! You will review your information once per school year to verify information is current and sign the forms. To register your student-athlete, please go to: https://hartford-mi.finalforms.com A couple of hints: 1. Bookmark this site or save it to your desktop on your mobile device or computer (do not Google search for it in the future as you will not go directly to the Hartford site). 2. Have required information available, such as medical history/health information, insurance company policy numbers, doctor, dentist and hospital information. This will make the registration time be more efficiently completed. 3. Parents will need to fill in your student’s e-mail address. FinalForms requires that the student’s @hpsmi.org email address can be used. Obtain this from your son/daughter – it is their last name and then first initial @hpsmi.org. Your student will then need to check their e-mail for information on how to complete their portion of the registration. 4. Attached is the ParentPlaybook-Hartford MI to help you with the online registration process. Please note, once you register, you will receive an e-mail to confirm your account, create a password, and then complete the required forms. Remember to print the sports physical form off of FinalForms and bring with you to the physician’s office.
